***умысел.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:умысел.html>у́мысел</a> (10159)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умысел.html>у́мысел</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">úmysel</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умысел.html>у́мысла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умысел.html>у́мыслы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умысел.html>у́мыслов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>design, intention
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:умысел.html>у́мыслом</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>úmyslom</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">intentionally; deliberately; of set purpose</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:умысел.html>у́мысла</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bez <b>úmysla</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">unintentionally</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>злой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:умысел.html>у́мысел</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zloj <b>úmysel</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">malicious intent</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>злым</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:умысел.html>у́мыслом</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">so zlym <b>úmyslom</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">with malicious intent; of malice prepense</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:умытый.html>умы́тый</a> (13862)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умытый.html>умы́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">umýtyj</span>)

***унёсший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:унести.html>унёсший</a> (3599)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унести.html>унёсший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">unjósšij</span>)

***унестись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:унестись.html>унести́сь</a> (25474)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унести.html>унести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унестись.html>унести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">unestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уноситься.html>уноси́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to leave quickly, to speed off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fly by <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be carried back <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of thoughts</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:универсал.html>универса́л</a> (26074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ūniversālis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:универсал.html>универса́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">universál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:универсал.html>универса́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:универсал.html>универса́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:универсал.html>универса́лов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">универса́лка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> jack of all trades, all-round craftsman, factotum</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> universalist</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">automotive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> estate car, station wagon</li>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:унижать.html>унижа́ть</a> (10072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:унизить.html>уни́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:унижать.html>унижа́ющий</a> (10072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>частичн.: <a href = vnd.unilang:оскорбить.html>оскорби́ть</a></li>
</ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уникальный.html>уника́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">unikálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уникальность.html>уника́льность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">unikálʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уникальность.html>уника́льности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уникальность.html>уника́льности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уникальность.html>уника́льностей</a></b>)
